 ) The Central Government once again went to the Supreme Court on Friday
 ek din pehle hi 122 2ji license radd karne kaa aadesh dene vaale nyaayalay ne shuukravaar ko sena pramukh kii umr se sambandhit vivaad main puri sarkari prakriya par hi sawaal uthaate hue kaha ki yah 'galat' maaloom padati he
 The court made this remark after hearing the petition of Army Chief General VK Singh
 maamle kii agali sunwaayee 10 farvari ko hogi
 The General has appealed in the petition to accept his date of birth as May 10, 1950 instead of May 10, 1951
 sena pramukh kii umr ko lekar yah vivaad sena kii do shakhaon main unki alag-alag janmatithi rahane ke kaaran he
 The Defense Ministry had dismissed General Singh's statutory complaint in this regard on December 30 last year, meaning that he would have to retire on May 31 this year
 isse pehle 21 july, 2011 ko bhi sarkaar ne sena pramukh kii janmatithi 10 may, 1950 hi maanane kaa aadesh jari kiya tha
 Both the government orders (december 30, 2011 and July 21, 2011) were based on the consultation of Attorney General GE Vahanvati
 is par nyaayamurti aaram lodha or nyaayamurti echel gokhale kii khandpeeth ne kaha ki general singh kii umr par liye gaye nirnay kii puri prakriya main 'prashasnic khami' maaloom padati he
 The question arises as to how the same legal officer can be consulted on the same issue twice
 puri prakriya hi 'galat' galat maaloom padati he
 The bench said, "our concern is not with the decision but the decision process, which seems to be wrong
" "tippaniyan The court also questioned Vahanvati, "once you have advised the government to decide on the law, how can you give your opinion in deciding the complaint again?" nyaayamurtiyon ne kaha, "samasya moulik he
 We are not talking about the decision being right or wrong, but the decision process is wrong
 " unhone kaha ki yah prakritik nyaay ke siddhant ke bhi khilaaf he
 He said that the Ministry of Defense can modify its order (order dated 30 December 2011) on independent legal consultation or the court will revoke it

 kohli or rohit kii dhamaakedaar batting ke baad kris gail ko jaldi nipataane ke baavjood team india ko haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa

 1
 At the beginning of his innings, the West Indies were in trouble, losing two big wickets from 19 balls

 3

 4
